            &lt;p class=&quot;refeditorFN&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Editor&#39;s note—&lt;/b&gt;
               The Charter, as amended, is set out herein as it appeared in the Charlottesville City
               Code of 1976. The basic Charter was enacted by Chapter 384 of the 1946 Acts of the
               General Assembly. Amendments are indicated by history notes appearing in parentheses
               (
               
               ) at the end of the amended section. The absence of such a note indicates that the
               section is derived, unamended, from Acts 1946, Chapter 384. Citations to the Code
               of Virginia have been made uniform. Words appearing in brackets [
               
               ] were added by the editor.
               &lt;/p&gt;
            
            &lt;p class=&quot;refstatelawFN&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;State Law reference— &lt;/b&gt;
               Governmental charters, Code of Virginia, &#167; 15.1-833 et seq.
               &lt;/p&gt;

            &lt;p class=&quot;refeditorFN&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Editor&#39;s note—&lt;/b&gt;
               Ord. of Dec. 1, 2003(1), amended Art. VII, in its entirety, to read as herein set
               out. Prior to inclusion of said ordinance, Art. VII pertained to similar subject matter.
